\DoxyCodeLine{01184             \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} size\_p\_to\_p0 = sqrt((p0.\mbox{\hyperlink{structPoint_a05dfe2dfbde813ad234b514f30e662f1}{x}} -\/ p.\mbox{\hyperlink{structPoint_a05dfe2dfbde813ad234b514f30e662f1}{x}})*(p0.\mbox{\hyperlink{structPoint_a05dfe2dfbde813ad234b514f30e662f1}{x}} -\/ p.\mbox{\hyperlink{structPoint_a05dfe2dfbde813ad234b514f30e662f1}{x}}) + (p0.\mbox{\hyperlink{structPoint_a6101960c8d2d4e8ea1d32c9234bbeb8d}{y}} -\/ p.\mbox{\hyperlink{structPoint_a6101960c8d2d4e8ea1d32c9234bbeb8d}{y}})*(p0.\mbox{\hyperlink{structPoint_a6101960c8d2d4e8ea1d32c9234bbeb8d}{y}} -\/ p.\mbox{\hyperlink{structPoint_a6101960c8d2d4e8ea1d32c9234bbeb8d}{y}}));}

\DoxyCodeLine{01188 }
\DoxyCodeLine{01189             \textcolor{comment}{/* calculating the tangent of half the angle directly using vector math */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01190             \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} t0 = \mbox{\hyperlink{Almog__Draw__Library_8h_a329be648e79affb9836f58c3b8cf397b}{adl\_tan\_half\_angle}}(p0, p1, p, size\_p\_to\_p0, size\_p\_to\_p1);}

\DoxyCodeLine{01194 }
\DoxyCodeLine{01195             \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} w0 = (t3 + t0) / size\_p\_to\_p0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01196             \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} w1 = (t0 + t1) / size\_p\_to\_p1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01197             \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} w2 = (t1 + t2) / size\_p\_to\_p2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01198             \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} w3 = (t2 + t3) / size\_p\_to\_p3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01199 }
\DoxyCodeLine{01200             \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} inv\_w\_tot = 1.0f / (w0 + w1 + w2 + w3);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01201             \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} alpha = w0 * inv\_w\_tot;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01202             \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} beta  = w1 * inv\_w\_tot;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01203             \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} gamma = w2 * inv\_w\_tot;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01204             \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} delta = w3 * inv\_w\_tot;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01205 }
